 The big networks save themselves from this struggle, but who has forgotten that era in the TV news industry, when suddenly the sensational news of astonishing and superstitious news took place and more or less all the channels got involved
 isamen koi do raay nahin ki patrakarita loktantr kaa ek mahatvapurn stambh he, par bharat main channelon kaa bijness model unhen zarurat se zyada bazaar par nirbhar kar detaa he
 There are countless problems of news channels here
 sabsakripshan se aamadani na ke baraabar he
 Competition is high and advertisers have many options, ie the bargaining power of revenue is less for channels and more for advertisers
 to kya edwartiging par had se zyada nirbhar hona, news media kii nishpakshta ko kathghare main khadaa karata he ? yahaan nirmal baba ke us daur ko yaad kariye, jab vah chaat-golgappas kii chatnee se gambheer se gambheer samasya kaa ilaaj de dete the
 When the news channels showed this dispute, they used to give ads on almost all the channels
 phir bhi yah khabar dikhaai gai
 Similarly, when news of pastides came out in Coca Cola and Pepsi, both these companies were the biggest advertisers in India
 iske baavjood vivaad ko anjaam tak pahunchaaya gaya
 That is, the business model is on one side and the fairness of the news media on the other side, but the danger of bias cannot be ruled out, plus all these examples cannot be applied to everyone
 aisi paristhitiyon main har channel kaa apana rukh hota he
 Self Regulation There are institutions to control every industry in our country
 telecom ke liye tri he
 SEBI is there for the stock market, but four pillars of society control themselves
 media swytt he
 The media has its own responsibility to decide social concerns
 hadein bhi swayan tay kii jaati hai
 Newspapers have their own institution
 tivi channelon kaa he enbie
 The NBA ie News Broadcasters Association is an association of private TV news and current affairs broadcasters
 yah puri tarah se sadasyon dwaara fundad he
 As of May 2016, 23 channels in the country were members of the NBA
 enbie kii website par kaamkaaj kaa vivaran kuch is prakaar he
 "the NBA presents the unified and trusted voice of the industry with the expanding media before the government
" enbie kaa doosraa pahalu he aatm nimantran, jiske liye vah code of athiks and broadcasting standerds ke jariye guidelins jari karata he
 These guidelines are valid for all member channels and they follow it
 quality control main enbie kii bhoomika ahm he, khaskar agar kisi channel ke content par kisi darshak ko aapatti he, to is shikaayat ko dur karne kaa jariya banataa he enbie
 Viewers can complain directly to that channel
 agar channel iskaa sangyaan nahin letaa yaa phir channel ke uthaaye kadam se darshak santusht nahin hota, to vah enbie se shikaayat kar saktaa he
 If the channel still does not respond within 14 days, the show can be issued a show cause notice by the NBA
 enbie main jeuri of piers sajaa tay karne kaa adhikaar rakhte hai
 It is a 9-member authority, headed by former Chief Justice (retd) JS Verma
 enbie ke paas adhikaar he galati karne vaale news channelon ko peshi ke liye bulaane kaa
 If the mistake is proved after the hearing, the NBA also has the right to warn
 galat khabar dikhaane yaa enbie ke disha-nirdesh kaa ulanghan karne ke maamle main ukt channel par fine bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he or unhen prime time main apni galati ke liye screen par likhit maafee maangane kaa farmaan sunaaya ja saktaa he
 News24 was forced to apologize on screen through an order dated 18 / 4 / 2012 for being found guilty of running a news promoting superstition
 isi tarah times nau par 11 / 3 / 2016 ke order ke jariye chhedhkhani ke aarope jhel rahe ek vyakti ke pakshpatpurna intervyuu ke liye pachaas hajaar kaa fine lagaaya gaya tha
 It was commented while writing the verdict, "the NBA realizes why the overjoyed media sometimes do injustice in trying to get justice
" iskaa aasaan jawaab he, tiarapy
 "in 8 years, the NBA has given a total of 41 decisions, but there are many news networks in the country who are not members of the NBA
" jo hai bhi, un par ek seemaa tak hi enbie kaa jor chal saktaa he
 Yet the attempt to stop messing with news in the era of marketism is commendable
 par niyantran ek ore he, duusari ore he daayitv
 Fear of punishment for making a mistake will control the quality, there are no two opinions, but now the time has come to take it a step further
 corporate soshal risponsibility kii tarah, media soshal risponsibility ek niyam ke taur par lagu kii ja sakati hai, taaki dilachasp shoj or rosemara kii khabaron ke saath logon ke hit kii khabaron ko bhi utani hi tavajjo di jaae
 For example, the disease of cancer in Punjab's land should not be shown as a special once in a year, but should be brought to its end
 kisi dur-daraaj ke skool main agar bachche bina chat ke khule main padhane ko majaboor hai, to keval sawaal na uthen, parantu javabdehi tay karne tak khabar chale
 It is not that media personnel do not want to do things that will bring a beautiful change in the society, but many times they are forced to face competition, because one channel shows the news of reform and the other sensational news at the same time, then whose loss will be there, Needless to say, but if MSR comes like CSR, then this rule will be applicable to competition too, as well as the audience who question the media
 That only sensational news is shown, that audience will also be judged that if only sensational news is not seen, what is the role of a journalist, a sinner, a journalist, a messenger? Whatever is happening around him, to convey the news to the people, or to tell what is happening, whether it is good or bad
 yah sawaal pechida he, kyonki agar tivi screen par aap ek bahu ko bujurg saas kii nirmam pitayee karte dekhte hai, to ankar kaa sanyam aapako pareshaan kar saktaa he
 If a politician in a show is trying to escape by lying white, then not stopping him would come under the purview of partiality
 lekin seemaa rekha bhala koun tay karegaa ? state of maharashtra VS
 Rajendra J
 gandhi [(1997) 8SCC 386] cese main sarvocch nyaayalay ne kaha, press, electronic media yaa janandolan kaa trial, rule of lau ke vipareet he
 The Supreme Court expressed anguish over the media trial in another case
 manu sharma VS
 In the case of State [(NCT of Delhi) - 2010 (6) SCC 1 (paras 301 and 299)], the court said, "the concept of innocence of an accused is a legal concept
" ise shuruyaat main hi media trial ke jariye nasht nahin karnaa chahie
 Especially when the investigation continues
 agar aisa kiya jaataa he, to yah nyaay ke buniyadi siddhanton ke viruddh hoga or aaropee ko samvidhan ke artical 21 ke tahat milane vaali suraksha kaa atikaraman bhi hoga
 The Freedom of Speech under Article 19 (1) (a) of the Constitution should be used with utmost care and attention so that the course of justice is not obstructed and the courts are not adversely affected by the cases under consideration
 adaalaton kii itani talkh tippaniyon ke baavjood midya trial kaa chalan jari rahata he
 In small-to-large cases, the culprits are fixed with a news break
 ho saktaa he ki saalon maamla chalane ke baad us shaks ko bizzat bari kar bhi diya jaae, par media trial main doshi paye jane ke baad us shaks kii saarvajanik chhavi khandit ho chuki hoti he
 Then, journalists should avoid taking a stand in any case, in this era of marketism when every moment of 24 hours a new picture is playing on the channels, straightforward news should be given? Then on live TV, when the instant commentary is going on, who has control over right and wrong and then even more important question is, who should decide the right and wrong? Theoretical explanation of the role of a journalist is not possible because a community To be fair, it would be toxic analysis for another
 jo khabar ek party ko sachhee lagegi, vah duusari party ke liye juthi hogi
 That is why we should return to following basic rules of journalism to avoid the glut of market news
 apane sorce se mil rahi khabaron kii sabhi pakshon se pushti karavaayi jaae
 While writing the news, facts should be given more importance than speculation and help of experts should be taken for comment
 hamen manjuur ho na ho, vakt badal chukaa he or badale hue vakt ne sab kuch badal diya he
 Now a newborn takes a month
 do saal ke bachche mobile, tablet, ypad main maharath hasil kar chuke hai
 If the mercury of the earth has been reversed, then journalism has also changed, the media of news and the likes of those watching the news
 lekin jo kabhi nahin badalanaa chahie, vah he ek patrkaar kii intaraatma, ek patrkaar kaa jameer, kyonki lakh aarope laga die jaaen, lakh niyam-kaayade tay kar die jaaen, jo sahi he or jo sach he, uski paribhaasha kabhi nahin badalegi

 eksrasij main airforce ke 181 ladaaku vimaan or helicopter hissaa le rahe hai or ise vayusena kaa shakti-pareekshan mana ja rahaa he
 Iron-fee exercise is taking place in the presence of Prime Minister Narendra Modi and President Pranab Mukherjee themselves
 yah yubhyas din or raat donon main hoga
 BS Dhanoa said that during the Kargil War, the Indian Air Force did not have the ability to conduct air-operations at night, but it would be shown in the iron-feast that after 16 years, the Air Force has the ability to conduct night-operations
 is yubhyas kaa moto (adarsh-vaakya) he apni sabak sikhaane kii kshamta kaa pradarshanhathiyaar sahi samay par sahi nishane par
